<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li><span class="homophones"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#homophone" title="Appendix:Glossary">Homophone</a>: <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/plain#English" title="plain">plain</a></span></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/planum#Latin" title="planum">plÄnum</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">flat surface</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a noun use of the neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/planus#Latin" title="planus">plÄnus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">plain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word was introduced in the 17th century to distinguish the geometrical senses from the other senses of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/plain#English" title="plain">plain</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/llano#English" title="llano">llano</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/piano#English" title="piano">piano</a></i><span class="serial-comma">,</span><span class="serial-and"> and</span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/plain#English" title="plain">plain</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparative" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planer#English" title="planer">planer</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#superlative" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planest#English" title="planest">planest</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a surface: <a href="/wiki/flat" title="flat">flat</a> or <a href="/wiki/level" title="level">level</a>.</li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planes#English" title="planes">planes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A level or flat surface.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/geometry" title="geometry">geometry</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A flat <a href="/wiki/surface" title="surface">surface</a> extending infinitely in all directions (e.g. horizontal or vertical plane).
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/anatomy" title="anatomy">anatomy</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An imaginary plane which divides the body into two portions.</li></ol></li>
<li>A level of existence or development.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">astral <b>plane</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A roughly flat, thin, often moveable structure used to create lateral force by the flow of air or water over its surface, found on aircraft, submarines, etc. <span class="use-with-mention">(Compare <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/wing#English" title="wing">wing</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/airfoil#English" title="airfoil">airfoil</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hydrofoil#English" title="hydrofoil">hydrofoil</a></span>.)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Unicode" title="Unicode">Unicode</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of 17 designated <a href="/wiki/range" title="range">ranges</a> of 2<sup>16</sup> (65,536) <a href="/wiki/sequential" title="sequential">sequential</a> <a href="/wiki/code_point" title="code point">code points</a> each.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyponyms">Hyponyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Hyponyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/real_plane#English" title="real plane">real plane</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/complex_plane#English" title="complex plane">complex plane</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/coronal_plane#English" title="coronal plane">coronal plane</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/frontal_plane#English" title="frontal plane">frontal plane</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sagittal_plane#English" title="sagittal plane">sagittal plane</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/transverse_plane#English" title="transverse plane">transverse plane</a></span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plane_(tool)" class="extiw" title="w:Plane (tool)">Plane (tool)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plane_(tool)" class="extiw" title="w:Plane (tool)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/plane#Middle_English" title="plane">plane</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/plaine#Middle_English" title="plaine">plaine</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/plaine#Old_French" title="plaine">plaine</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/plana#Latin" title="plana">plÄna</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">planing tool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg/200px-Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="154" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg/300px-Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg/400px-Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1441" data-file-height="1110"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Stanley_No10_carriagemakers_rebate_plane.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>a <a href="/wiki/rebate_plane" title="rebate plane">rebate plane</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planes#English" title="planes">planes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/tool" title="tool">tool</a> for <a href="/wiki/smooth" title="smooth">smoothing</a> <a href="/wiki/wood" title="wood">wood</a> by removing thin layers from the <a href="/wiki/surface" title="surface">surface</a>.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#clipping" title="Appendix:Glossary">Clipping</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/aeroplane#English" title="aeroplane">aeroplane</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planes#English" title="planes">planes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An <a href="/wiki/airplane" title="airplane">airplane</a>; an <a href="/wiki/aeroplane" title="aeroplane">aeroplane</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;â–¼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> September 6,  Tom Cheshire,  â€œ<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/technology/2013/aug/25/solar-power-transport-travel-technology">Solar-powered travel</a>â€, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Guardian_Weekly" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Guardian Weekly">The Guardian Weekly</a></cite>, volume 189, number 13, page 34:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <b>plane</b> is travelling impossibly slowly â€“ 30km an hour â€“ when it gently noses up and leaves the ground. With air beneath them, the rangy wings seem to gain strength; the fuselage that on the ground seemed flimsy becomes elegant, like a crane vaunting in flight. It seems not to fly, though, so much as float.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/entomology" title="entomology">entomology</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of various <a href="/wiki/nymphalid" title="nymphalid">nymphalid</a> butterflies, of various genera, having a slow gliding flight.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/aeroplane#English" title="aeroplane">aeroplane</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/entomology" title="entomology">entomology</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The butterfly <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bindahara_phocides" class="extiw" title="w:Bindahara phocides">Bindahara phocides</a></i>, family <a href="/wiki/Lycaenidae" title="Lycaenidae">Lycaenidae</a>, of Asia and Australasia.</li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planes#English" title="planes">planes</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planing#English" title="planing">planing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planed#English" title="planed">planed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move in a way that lifts the <a href="/wiki/bow" title="bow">bow</a> of a <a href="/wiki/boat" title="boat">boat</a> out of the <a href="/wiki/water" title="water">water</a>.</li>
<li>To <a href="/wiki/glide" title="glide">glide</a> or <a href="/wiki/soar" title="soar">soar</a>.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Etymology 4">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/plane#Middle_English" title="plane">plane</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/plane#Old_French" title="plane">plane</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/platanus#Latin" title="platanus">platanus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%80%CE%BB%CE%AC%CF%84%CE%B1%CE%BD%CE%BF%CF%82#Ancient_Greek" title="Ï€Î»Î¬Ï„Î±Î½Î¿Ï‚">Ï€Î»Î¬Ï„Î±Î½Î¿Ï‚</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plÃ¡tanos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%80%CE%BB%CE%B1%CF%84%CF%8D%CF%82#Ancient_Greek" title="Ï€Î»Î±Ï„ÏÏ‚">Ï€Î»Î±Ï„ÏÏ‚</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">platÃºs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">wide, broad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=plane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">plane</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/planes#English" title="planes">planes</a></b>)
</p>
